
kuat_system_selector_initialization = {
	optimize_memory
	set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 1 }
	set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_star_classes_page value = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "has_real_space_mod" } }
		set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_star_classes_page_total value = 2 }
	}
	else = { set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_star_classes_page_total value = 6 } }
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		set_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 2 }			# Page1.1 means system without space_owner, Page1.2 means unknown targets.
		set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 1 }
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { OR = {
			AND = { is_same_value = root count_system_within_border = { count > 0 } }
			AND = { NOT = { is_same_value = root } has_communications = root count_system_within_border = { count > 0 } }
			is_eternal_faction = yes
		} }
		set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country
		event_target:global_event_country = {
			change_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 10 } }
				set_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 1 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 1 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 1 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 2 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 2 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 3 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 3 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 4 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 4 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 5 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 5 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 6 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 6 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 7 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 7 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 8 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 8 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_countries value = 9 } } kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = { kuat_country_seq = 9 } }
		}
	}
}
kuat_system_selector_load_page_country = {
	optimize_memory
	kuat_system_selector_clear_targets_country = yes
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 1 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_1 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 1 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 2 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_2 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 2 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 3 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_3 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 3 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 4 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_4 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 4 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 5 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_5 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 5 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 6 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_6 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 6 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 7 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_7 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 7 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 8 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_8 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 8 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 9 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_9 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 9 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 10 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_10 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 10 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 11 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_11 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 11 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 12 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_12 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 12 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 13 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_13 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 13 } }

	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 15 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_15 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 15 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 16 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_16 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 16 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 17 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_17 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 17 } }
	}

		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_18 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 18 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 19 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_19 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 19 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 20 } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_20 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 20 } }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 21 } }

	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page value = 22 } }

		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_24 } kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = { kuat_page_seq = 24 } }

kuat_system_selector_load_page_country_get_targets = {
	optimize_memory
	if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_1 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_1 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_2 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_2 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_3 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_3 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_4 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_4 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_5 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_5 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_6 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_6 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_7 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_7 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_8 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_8 }
	else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_9 } save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_country_9 }
}
kuat_system_selector_clear_targets_country = {
	optimize_memory
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_1 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_1 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_2 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_2 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_3 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_3 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_4 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_4 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_5 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_5 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_6 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_6 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_7 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_7 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_8 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_8 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_9 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_country_9 }
}
kuat_system_selector_after_effect = {
	optimize_memory
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country }
		remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country
		remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected
		kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag = yes
	}
	every_system = {
		limit = { has_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_selected_system }
		remove_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_selected_system
	}
	kuat_system_selector_clear_targets_country = yes
	kuat_system_selector_clear_selected_country_flag = yes
	kuat_system_selector_clear_selected_star_class_flag = yes
	kuat_system_selector_clear_selected_star_country_flag = yes
	remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_disable_country_triggers
	remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_disable_star_classes_triggers
	remove_global_flag = kuat_system_selector_initialized
	set_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_selected_systems value = 0 }
	clear_variable = kuat_num_system_selector_selected_systems
}
# Scope: global_event_country
# Prev: Target Country
kuat_system_selector_set_target_country_flag = {
	optimize_memory
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 1 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_1 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_1_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 2 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_2 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_2_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 3 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_3 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_3_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 4 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_4 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_4_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 5 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_5 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_5_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 6 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_6 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_6_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 7 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_7 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_7_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 8 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_8 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_8_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 9 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_9 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_9_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 10 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_10 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_10_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 11 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_11 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_11_$kuat_country_seq$ } }

	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_countries_page_total value = 14 } } prev = { set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_14 set_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_14_$kuat_country_seq$ } }

}
kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag = {
	optimize_memory
	switch = {
		trigger = has_country_flag
		kuat_system_selector_country_1 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 1 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_2 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 2 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_3 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 3 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_4 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 4 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_5 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 5 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_6 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 6 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_7 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 7 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_8 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 8 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_9 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 9 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_10 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 10 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_11 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 11 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_12 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 12 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_13 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 13 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_14 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 14 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_15 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 15 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_16 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 16 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_17 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 17 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_18 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 18 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_19 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 19 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_20 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 20 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_21 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 21 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_22 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 22 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_23 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 23 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_24 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 24 } }
		kuat_system_selector_country_25 = { kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = { kuat_page_seq = 25 } }
	}
}
kuat_system_selector_clear_target_country_flag_1 = {
	optimize_memory
	remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$
	remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_1
	remove_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_page_seq$_2

kuat_system_selector_select_unknown_country = {
	optimize_memory
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1_2 } }
		set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1
		set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1_2
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOR = { is_same_value = root has_communications = root } }
			set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected
		}
	}
	else = {
		remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1
		remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1_2
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOR = { is_same_value = root has_communications = root } }
			remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected
		}
	}
}

kuat_system_selector_select_country_1 = {
	optimize_memory
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$_$kuat_country_seq$ } }
		if = {
			limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_country_seq$ }
			event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_country_seq$ = { set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected }
		}
		set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$
		set_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$_$kuat_country_seq$
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_country_seq$ }
			event_target:kuat_system_selector_country_$kuat_country_seq$ = { remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected }
		}
		remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$
		remove_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$_$kuat_country_seq$
	}
}
kuat_system_selector_select_star_class = {

		set_country_flag = kuat_star_classes_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$_$kuat_sc_seq$
	}
	else = {
		remove_country_flag = kuat_star_classes_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$
		remove_country_flag = kuat_star_classes_list_selected_$kuat_page_seq$_$kuat_sc_seq$
	}
}

kuat_select_system_effect = {
	optimize_memory
	set_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 0 }
	set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_marked_page value = 1 }
	set_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_marked_pages_total value = 1 }
	every_system = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				prev = { has_country_flag = kuat_system_selector_disable_country_triggers }
				AND = {
					NOT = { exists = space_owner }
					prev = { has_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected_1_1 }
				}
				AND = {
					exists = space_owner
					space_owner = { has_country_flag = kuat_countries_list_selected }
				}
			}
			kuat_star_classes_check = yes
		}
		set_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_marked
		prev = {
			change_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 13 } }
				set_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = kuat_system_selector_marked_pages_total value = 1 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 1 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 1 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 2 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 2 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 3 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 3 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 4 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 4 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 5 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 5 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 6 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 6 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 7 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 7 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 8 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 8 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 9 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 9 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 10 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 10 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 11 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 11 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_marks value = 12 } } kuat_select_system_set_star_flags = { kuat_system_seq = 12 } }
		}
	}
}

kuat_set_system_event_targets_1 = {
	optimize_memory
	every_system = {
		limit = { has_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$ }
		switch = {
			trigger = has_star_flag
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_1 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_1 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_2 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_2 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_3 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_3 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_4 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_4 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_5 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_5 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_6 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_6 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_7 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_7 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_8 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_8 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_9 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_9 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_10 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_10 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_11 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_11 }
			kuat_system_selector_marked_$kuat_page_seq$_12 = { save_global_event_target_as = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_12 }
		}
	}
}
kuat_clear_system_event_targets = {
	optimize_memory
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_1 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_1 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_2 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_2 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_3 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_3 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_4 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_4 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_5 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_5 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_6 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_6 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_7 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_7 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_8 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_8 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_9 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_9 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_10 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_10 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_11 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_11 }
	if = { limit = { exists = event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_12 } clear_global_event_target = kuat_system_selector_marked_system_12 }
}
kuat_selected_system_effect = {
	optimize_memory
	event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_$kuat_system_seq$ = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_selected_system } }
			root = { change_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_selected_systems value = 1 } }
			set_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_selected_system
			prev = { kuat_selected_system_effect_1 = { kuat_system_seq = $kuat_system_seq$ } }
		}
		else = {
			root = { subtract_variable = { which = kuat_num_system_selector_selected_systems value = 1 } }
			remove_star_flag = kuat_system_selector_selected_system
			prev = { kuat_selected_system_effect_1_alt = { kuat_system_seq = $kuat_system_seq$ } }
		}
	}
}

kuat_system_selector_system_target_loc = {
	event_target:kuat_system_selector_marked_system_$kuat_system_seq$ = {
		if = { limit = { exists = space_owner } custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.$kuat_system_seq$.space_owner" }
		else = { custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.$kuat_system_seq$.space_owner_alt" }
		if = { limit = { is_capital_system = yes } custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.is_capital" }
		if = { limit = { any_system_planet = { is_colony = yes } } custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.is_colony" }
		if = { limit = { has_natural_wormhole = yes } custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.wormhole" }
		if = {
			limit = { has_any_megastructure = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { any_system_megastructure = { OR = {
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_0
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_final
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_ruined
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_restored
				} } }
				custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.gateway"
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_system_megastructure = { is_megastructure_type = lgate_base } }
				custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.lgate"
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_system_megastructure = { NOR = {
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_0
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_final
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_ruined
					is_megastructure_type = gateway_restored
					is_megastructure_type = lgate_base
				} } }
				custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.megastructure"
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { kuat_is_sc_eternal_fleet = yes } custom_tooltip = "kuat_system_selector.eternal_fleet" }
	}
}
